## Global Constraints

- `global.no_hermes_core_patch` (critical): Phase 8 must not modify Hermes core files.
- `global.no_patch_generation` (critical): Phase 8 must not generate source patches.
- `global.feature_flag_first` (high): Future runnable integration must be gated by HERMES_EXT_* feature flags.
- `global.kill_switch_required` (critical): Any future integration must honor HERMES_EXT_KILL_SWITCH.
- `global.shadow_before_native` (critical): Shadow harness validation must precede any native Hermes integration.

## Warnings

- Spec contains forbidden entries; these are blocked and design-only.

## Non-negotiable Rule

This document is a design matrix only. It must not be interpreted as approval to patch Hermes core files.
